Code from ../main.py:67 >>>>>
def pred(derivation):
	"""
	Keyword arguments:
	d --- a derivation graph object
	"""
	for g in derivation.right:
		if g.exactMass >= max_mass_limit:
			return False
		for allowed in allowed_structs:
			if g.monomorphism(allowed) > 0:
				return True
		# Allow masses only lower than a certain maximum
		for fb in forbidden:
			if fb.monomorphism(g, labelSettings=
			LabelSettings(LabelType.Term, LabelRelation.Specialisation)) > 0:
				return False
		#print(g)
	return True

Code from ../main.py:67 >>>>>
def pred(derivation):
	"""
	Keyword arguments:
	d --- a derivation graph object
	"""
	for g in derivation.right:
		if g.exactMass >= max_mass_limit:
			return False
		for allowed in allowed_structs:
			if g.monomorphism(allowed) > 0:
				return True
		# Allow masses only lower than a certain maximum
		for fb in forbidden:
			if fb.monomorphism(g, labelSettings=
			LabelSettings(LabelType.Term, LabelRelation.Specialisation)) > 0:
				return False
		#print(g)
	return True

Code from ../main.py:67 >>>>>
def pred(derivation):
	"""
	Keyword arguments:
	d --- a derivation graph object
	"""
	for g in derivation.right:
		if g.exactMass >= max_mass_limit:
			return False
		for allowed in allowed_structs:
			if g.monomorphism(allowed) > 0:
				return True
		# Allow masses only lower than a certain maximum
		for fb in forbidden:
			if fb.monomorphism(g, labelSettings=
			LabelSettings(LabelType.Term, LabelRelation.Specialisation)) > 0:
				return False
		#print(g)
	return True

Code from ../main.py:67 >>>>>
def pred(derivation):
	"""
	Keyword arguments:
	d --- a derivation graph object
	"""
	for g in derivation.right:
		if g.exactMass >= max_mass_limit:
			return False
		for allowed in allowed_structs:
			if g.monomorphism(allowed) > 0:
				return True
		# Allow masses only lower than a certain maximum
		for fb in forbidden:
			if fb.monomorphism(g, labelSettings=
			LabelSettings(LabelType.Term, LabelRelation.Specialisation)) > 0:
				return False
		#print(g)
	return True
